allows applications to provide context for LLMs in a standardized way, separating the concerns of providing context from the actual LLM interaction. This Python SDK implements the full MCP specification, making it easy to:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBuild MCP clients that can connect to any MCP server\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCreate MCP servers that expose resources, prompts and tools\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUse standard transports like stdio, SSE, and Streamable 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe \u003ca href=\"https://modelcontextprotocol.io\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eModel Context Protocol (MCP)\u003c/a\u003e lets you build servers that expose data and functionality to LLM applications in a secure, standardized way. Think of it like a web API, but specifically designed for LLM interactions. MCP servers can:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eExpose data through \u003cstrong\u003eResources\u003c/strong\u003e (think of these sort of like GET endpoints; they are used to load information into the LLM's context)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eProvide functionality through \u003cstrong\u003eTools\u003c/strong\u003e (sort of like POST endpoints; they are used to execute code or otherwise produce a side effect)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDefine interaction patterns through \u003cstrong\u003ePrompts\u003c/strong\u003e (reusable templates for LLM interactions)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAnd more!\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch4 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eStructured Output\u003c/h4\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-structured-output\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Structured Output\" href=\"#structured-output\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTools will return structured results by default, if their return type\nannotation is compatible. Otherwise, they will return unstructured results.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eStructured output supports these return types:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePydantic models (BaseModel subclasses)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTypedDicts\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDataclasses and other classes with type hints\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003edict[str, T]\u003c/code\u003e (where T is any JSON-serializable type)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePrimitive types (str, int, float, bool, bytes, None) - wrapped in \u003ccode\u003e{\"result\": value}\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eGeneric types (list, tuple, Union, Optional, etc.) - wrapped in \u003ccode\u003e{\"result\": value}\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eClasses without type hints cannot be serialized for structured output. Only\nclasses with properly annotated attributes will be converted to Pydantic models\nfor schema generation and validation.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eStructured results are automatically validated against the output schema\ngenerated from the annotation. This ensures the tool returns well-typed,\nvalidated data that clients can easily process.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNote:\u003c/strong\u003e For backward compatibility, unstructured results are also\nreturned. Unstructured results are provided for backward compatibility\nwith previous versions of the MCP specification, and are quirks-compatible\nwith previous versions of FastMCP in the current version of the SDK.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNote:\u003c/strong\u003e In cases where a tool function's return type annotation\ncauses the tool to be classified as structured \u003cem\u003eand this is undesirable\u003c/em\u003e,\nthe  classification can be suppressed by passing \u003ccode\u003estructured_output=False\u003c/code\u003e\nto the \u003ccode\u003e@tool\u003c/code\u003e decorator.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"from mcp.server.fastmcp import FastMCP\nfrom pydantic import BaseModel, Field\nfrom typing import TypedDict\n\nmcp = FastMCP(\u0026quot;Weather Service\u0026quot;)\n\n\n# Using Pydantic models for rich structured data\nclass WeatherData(BaseModel):\n    temperature: float = Field(description=\u0026quot;Temperature in Celsius\u0026quot;)\n    humidity: float = Field(description=\u0026quot;Humidity percentage\u0026quot;)\n    condition: str\n    wind_speed: float\n\n\n@mcp.tool()\ndef get_weather(city: str) -\u0026gt; WeatherData:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Get structured weather data\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    return WeatherData(\n        temperature=22.5, humidity=65.0, condition=\u0026quot;partly cloudy\u0026quot;, wind_speed=12.3\n    )\n\n\n# Using TypedDict for simpler structures\nclass LocationInfo(TypedDict):\n    latitude: float\n    longitude: float\n    name: str\n\n\n@mcp.tool()\ndef get_location(address: str) -\u0026gt; LocationInfo:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Get location coordinates\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    return LocationInfo(latitude=51.5074, longitude=-0.1278, name=\u0026quot;London, UK\u0026quot;)\n\n\n# Using dict[str, Any] for flexible schemas\n@mcp.tool()\ndef get_statistics(data_type: str) -\u0026gt; dict[str, float]:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Get various statistics\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    return {\u0026quot;mean\u0026quot;: 42.5, \u0026quot;median\u0026quot;: 40.0, \u0026quot;std_dev\u0026quot;: 5.2}\n\n\n# Ordinary classes with type hints work for structured output\nclass UserProfile:\n    name: str\n    age: int\n    email: str | None = None\n\n    def __init__(self, name: str, age: int, email: str | None = None):\n        self.name = name\n        self.age = age\n        self.email = email\n\n\n@mcp.tool()\ndef get_user(user_id: str) -\u0026gt; UserProfile:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Get user profile - returns structured data\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    return UserProfile(name=\u0026quot;Alice\u0026quot;, age=30, email=\u0026quot;alice@example.com\u0026quot;)\n\n\n# Classes WITHOUT type hints cannot be used for structured output\nclass UntypedConfig:\n    def __init__(self, setting1, setting2):\n        self.setting1 = setting1\n        self.setting2 = setting2\n\n\n@mcp.tool()\ndef get_config() -\u0026gt; UntypedConfig:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;This returns unstructured output - no This example shows an Elicitation during a Tool Call:\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"from pydantic import BaseModel, Field\n\nfrom mcp.server.fastmcp import Context, FastMCP\n\nmcp = FastMCP(name=\u0026quot;Elicitation Example\u0026quot;)\n\n\nclass BookingPreferences(BaseModel):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Schema for collecting user preferences.\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n\n    checkAlternative: bool = Field(description=\u0026quot;Would you like to check another date?\u0026quot;)\n    alternativeDate: str = Field(\n        default=\u0026quot;2024-12-26\u0026quot;,\n        description=\u0026quot;Alternative date (YYYY-MM-DD)\u0026quot;,\n    )\n\n\n@mcp.tool()\nasync def book_table(\n    date: str,\n    time: str,\n    party_size: int,\n    ctx: Context,\n) -\u0026gt; str:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Book a table with date availability check.\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    # Check if date is available\n    if date == \u0026quot;2024-12-25\u0026quot;:\n        # Date unavailable - ask user for alternative\n        result = await ctx.elicit(\n            message=(f\u0026quot;No tables available for {party_size} on {date}. Would you like to try another date?\u0026quot;),\n            schema=BookingPreferences,\n        )\n\n        if result.action == \u0026quot;accept\u0026quot; and result.data:\n            if result.data.checkAlternative:\n                return f\u0026quot;[SUCCESS] Booked for {result.data.alternativeDate}\u0026quot;\n            return \u0026quot;[CANCELLED] No booking made\u0026quot;\n        return \u0026quot;[CANCELLED] Booking cancelled\u0026quot;\n\n    # Date available\n    return f\u0026quot;[SUCCESS] Booked for {date} at {time}\u0026quot;\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003efrom\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003epydantic\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ename\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"Elicitation Example\"\u003c/span\u003e)\n\n\n\u003cspan resources.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003emcp.server.auth\u003c/code\u003e implements OAuth 2.1 resource server functionality, where MCP servers act as Resource Servers (RS) 9728 (Protected Resource Metadata) for AS discovery.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eMCP servers can use authentication by providing an implementation of the dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNote\u003c/strong\u003e: SSE transport is being superseded by \u003ca href=\"https://modelcontextprotocol.io/specification/2025-03-26/basic/transports#streamable-http\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eStreamable HTTP transport\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eBy default, SSE servers are mounted at \u003ccode\u003e/sse\u003c/code\u003e and Streamable HTTP servers are mounted at \u003ccode\u003e/mcp\u003c/code\u003e. You can customize these paths using the methods described below.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can mount the SSE server to an existing ASGI server using the \u003ccode\u003esse_app\u003c/code\u003e method. This allows you to integrate the SSE server with other ASGI applications.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"from starlette.applications import Starlette\nfrom starlette.routing import Mount, Host\nfrom mcp.server.fastmcp import FastMCP\n\n\nmcp = FastMCP(\u0026quot;My App\u0026quot;)\n\n# Mount the SSE server to the existing ASGI server\napp = Starlette(\n    routes=[\n        Mount('/', app=mcp.sse_app()),\n    ]\n)\n\n# or dynamically mount as viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe low-level server supports structured output for tools, allowing you to return both human-readable content and machine-readable structured data. Tools can define an \u003ccode\u003eoutputSchema\u003c/code\u003e to validate their structured output:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"from types import Any\n\nimport mcp.types as types\nfrom mcp.server.lowlevel import Server\n\nserver = Server(\u0026quot;example-server\u0026quot;)\n\n\n@server.list_tools()\nasync def list_tools() -\u0026gt; list[types.Tool]:\n    return [\n        types.Tool(\n            name=\u0026quot;calculate\u0026quot;,\n            description=\u0026quot;Perform mathematical calculations\u0026quot;,\n            inputSchema={\n                \u0026quot;type\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;object\u0026quot;,\n                \u0026quot;properties\u0026quot;: {\n                    \u0026quot;expression\u0026quot;: {\u0026quot;type\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;string\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;description\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;Math expression\u0026quot;}\n                },\n                \u0026quot;required\u0026quot;: [\u0026quot;expression\u0026quot;],\n            },\n            outputSchema={\n                \u0026quot;type\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;object\u0026quot;,\n                \u0026quot;properties\u0026quot;: {\n                    \u0026quot;result\u0026quot;: {\u0026quot;type\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;number\u0026quot;},\n                    \u0026quot;expression\u0026quot;: {\u0026quot;type\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;string\u0026quot;},\n                },\n                \u0026quot;required\u0026quot;: [\u0026quot;result\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;expression\u0026quot;],\n            },\n        )\n    ]\n\n\n@server.call_tool()\nasync def call_tool(name: str, arguments: dict[str, Any]) -\u0026gt; dict[str, Any]:\n    if name == \u0026quot;calculate\u0026quot;:\n        expression = arguments[\u0026quot;expression\u0026quot;]\n        try:\n            result = eval(expression)  # Use a safe math parser\n            structured = {\u0026quot;result\u0026quot;: result, \u0026quot;expression\u0026quot;: expression}\n\n            # low-level server will validate structured output against the tool's\n            # output schema, and automatically serialize it into a TextContent block\n            # for backwards compatibility with pre-2025-06-18 clients.\n            return structured\n        except Exception as e:\n            raise ValueError(f\u0026quot;Calculation error: {str(e)}\u0026quot;)\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan          \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"required\"\u003c/span\u003e: [\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"result\"\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"expression\"\u003c/span\u003e],\n return data in three ways:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eContent only\u003c/strong\u003e: Return a list of content blocks (default behavior before spec revision 2025-06-18)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eStructured data only\u003c/strong\u003e: Return a dictionary that will be serialized to JSON (Introduced in spec revision 2025-06-18)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBoth\u003c/strong\u003e: Return a tuple of (content, structured_data) preferred option to use for backwards compatibility\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhen an \u003ccode\u003eoutputSchema\u003c/code\u003e is defined, the server automatically validates the structured output against the schema. <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Overview</h2><a id="user-content-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Overview" href="#overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Model Context Protocol allows applications to provide context for LLMs in a standardized way, separating the concerns of providing context from the actual LLM interaction. This Python SDK implements the full MCP specification, making it easy to:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Build MCP clients that can connect to any MCP server</li>
<li>Create MCP servers that expose resources, prompts and tools</li>
<li>Use standard transports like stdio, SSE, and Streamable HTTP</li>
<li>Handle all MCP protocol messages and lifecycle events</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h2><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Adding MCP to your python project</h3><a id="user-content-adding-mcp-to-your-python-project" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Adding MCP to your python project" href="#adding-mcp-to-your-python-project"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We recommend using <a href="https://docs.astral.sh/uv/" rel="nofollow">uv</a> to manage your Python projects.</p>
<p dir="auto">If you haven't created a uv-managed project yet, create one:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="uv init mcp-server-demo
cd mcp-server-demo"><pre>uv init mcp-server-demo
<span class="pl-c1">cd</span> mcp-server-demo</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Then add MCP to your project dependencies:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="uv add &quot;mcp[cli]&quot;"><pre>uv add <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>mcp[cli]<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Alternatively, for projects using pip for dependencies:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pip install &quot;mcp[cli]&quot;"><pre>pip install <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>mcp[cli]<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Running the standalone MCP development tools</h3><a id="user-content-running-the-standalone-mcp-development-tools" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Running the standalone MCP development tools" href="#running-the-standalone-mcp-development-tools"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To run the mcp command with uv:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="uv run mcp"><pre>uv run mcp</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quickstart</h2><a id="user-content-quickstart" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quickstart" href="#quickstart"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Let's create a simple MCP server that exposes a calculator tool and some data:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# server.py
from mcp.server.fastmcp import FastMCP

# Create an MCP server
mcp = FastMCP(&quot;Demo&quot;)


# Add an addition tool
@mcp.tool()
def sum(a: int, b: int) -&gt; int:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Add two numbers&quot;&quot;&quot;
    return a + b


# Add a dynamic greeting resource
@mcp.resource(&quot;greeting://{name}&quot;)
def get_greeting(name: str) -&gt; str:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Get a personalized greeting&quot;&quot;&quot;
    return f&quot;Hello, {name}!&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-c"># server.py</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-s1">server</span>.<span class="pl-s1">fastmcp</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">FastMCP</span>

<span class="pl-c"># Create an MCP server</span>
<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">FastMCP</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Demo"</span>)


<span class="pl-c"># Add an addition tool</span>
<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">tool</span>()</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">sum</span>(<span class="pl-s1">a</span>: <span class="pl-smi">int</span>, <span class="pl-s1">b</span>: <span class="pl-smi">int</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">int</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Add two numbers"""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span>


<span class="pl-c"># Add a dynamic greeting resource</span>
<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">resource</span>(<span class="pl-s">"greeting://{name}"</span>)</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_greeting</span>(<span class="pl-s1">name</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">str</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Get a personalized greeting"""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">f"Hello, <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>!"</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">You can install this server in <a href="https://claude.ai/download" rel="nofollow">Claude Desktop</a> and interact with it right away by running:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="uv run mcp install server.py"><pre>uv run mcp install server.py</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Alternatively, you can test it with the MCP Inspector:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="uv run mcp dev server.py"><pre>uv run mcp dev server.py</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What is MCP?</h2><a id="user-content-what-is-mcp" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What is MCP?" href="#what-is-mcp"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <a href="https://modelcontextprotocol.io" rel="nofollow">Model Context Protocol (MCP)</a> lets you build servers that expose data and functionality to LLM applications in a secure, standardized way. Think of it like a web API, but specifically designed for LLM interactions. MCP servers can:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Expose data through <strong>Resources</strong> (think of these sort of like GET endpoints; they are used to load information into the LLM's context)</li>
<li>Provide functionality through <strong>Tools</strong> (sort of like POST endpoints; they are used to execute code or otherwise produce a side effect)</li>
<li>Define interaction patterns through <strong>Prompts</strong> (reusable templates for LLM interactions)</li>
<li>And more!</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Core Concepts</h2><a id="user-content-core-concepts" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Core Concepts" href="#core-concepts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Server</h3><a id="user-content-server" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Server" href="#server"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The FastMCP server is your core interface to the MCP protocol. It handles connection management, protocol compliance, and message routing:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Add lifespan support for startup/shutdown with strong typing
from contextlib import asynccontextmanager
from collections.abc import AsyncIterator
from dataclasses import dataclass

from fake_database import Database  # Replace with your actual DB type

from mcp.server.fastmcp import FastMCP

# Create a named server
mcp = FastMCP(&quot;My App&quot;)

# Specify dependencies for deployment and development
mcp = FastMCP(&quot;My App&quot;, dependencies=[&quot;pandas&quot;, &quot;numpy&quot;])


@dataclass
class AppContext:
    db: Database


@asynccontextmanager
async def app_lifespan(server: FastMCP) -&gt; AsyncIterator[AppContext]:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Manage application lifecycle with type-safe context&quot;&quot;&quot;
    # Initialize on startup
    db = await Database.connect()
    try:
        yield AppContext(db=db)
    finally:
        # Cleanup on shutdown
        await db.disconnect()


# Pass lifespan to server
mcp = FastMCP(&quot;My App&quot;, lifespan=app_lifespan)


# Access type-safe lifespan context in tools
@mcp.tool()
def query_db() -&gt; str:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Tool that uses initialized resources&quot;&quot;&quot;
    ctx = mcp.get_context()
    db = ctx.request_context.lifespan_context[&quot;db&quot;]
    return db.query()"><pre><span class="pl-c"># Add lifespan support for startup/shutdown with strong typing</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">contextlib</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">asynccontextmanager</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">collections</span>.<span class="pl-s1">abc</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">AsyncIterator</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">dataclasses</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">dataclass</span>

<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">fake_database</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">Database</span>  <span class="pl-c"># Replace with your actual DB type</span>

<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-s1">server</span>.<span class="pl-s1">fastmcp</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">FastMCP</span>

<span class="pl-c"># Create a named server</span>
<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">FastMCP</span>(<span class="pl-s">"My App"</span>)

<span class="pl-c"># Specify dependencies for deployment and development</span>
<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">FastMCP</span>(<span class="pl-s">"My App"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">dependencies</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[<span class="pl-s">"pandas"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"numpy"</span>])


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">dataclass</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">AppContext</span>:
    <span class="pl-s1">db</span>: <span class="pl-smi">Database</span>


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">asynccontextmanager</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">app_lifespan</span>(<span class="pl-s1">server</span>: <span class="pl-smi">FastMCP</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-v">AsyncIterator</span>[<span class="pl-smi">AppContext</span>]:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Manage application lifecycle with type-safe context"""</span>
    <span class="pl-c"># Initialize on startup</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">db</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-v">Database</span>.<span class="pl-c1">connect</span>()
    <span class="pl-k">try</span>:
        <span class="pl-k">yield</span> <span class="pl-en">AppContext</span>(<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">db</span>)
    <span class="pl-k">finally</span>:
        <span class="pl-c"># Cleanup on shutdown</span>
        <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">db</span>.<span class="pl-c1">disconnect</span>()


<span class="pl-c"># Pass lifespan to server</span>
<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">FastMCP</span>(<span class="pl-s">"My App"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">lifespan</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">app_lifespan</span>)


<span class="pl-c"># Access type-safe lifespan context in tools</span>
<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">tool</span>()</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">query_db</span>() <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">str</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Tool that uses initialized resources"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">ctx</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get_context</span>()
    <span class="pl-s1">db</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">ctx</span>.<span class="pl-c1">request_context</span>.<span class="pl-c1">lifespan_context</span>[<span class="pl-s">"db"</span>]
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">db</span>.<span class="pl-c1">query</span>()</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Resources</h3><a id="user-content-resources" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Resources" href="#resources"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Resources are how you expose data to LLMs. They're similar to GET endpoints in a REST API - they provide data but shouldn't perform significant computation or have side effects:</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from mcp.server.fastmcp import FastMCP

mcp = FastMCP(name=&quot;Resource Example&quot;)


@mcp.resource(&quot;file://documents/{name}&quot;)
def read_document(name: str) -&gt; str:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Read a document by name.&quot;&quot;&quot;
    # This would normally read from disk
    return f&quot;Content of {name}&quot;


@mcp.resource(&quot;config://settings&quot;)
def get_settings() -&gt; str:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Get application settings.&quot;&quot;&quot;
    return &quot;&quot;&quot;{
  &quot;theme&quot;: &quot;dark&quot;,
  &quot;language&quot;: &quot;en&quot;,
  &quot;debug&quot;: false
}&quot;&quot;&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-s1">server</span>.<span class="pl-s1">fastmcp</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">FastMCP</span>

<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">FastMCP</span>(<span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Resource Example"</span>)


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">resource</span>(<span class="pl-s">"file://documents/{name}"</span>)</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">read_document</span>(<span class="pl-s1">name</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">str</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Read a document by name."""</span>
    <span class="pl-c"># This would normally read from disk</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">f"Content of <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">resource</span>(<span class="pl-s">"config://settings"</span>)</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_settings</span>() <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">str</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Get application settings."""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">"""{</span>
<span class="pl-s">  "theme": "dark",</span>
<span class="pl-s">  "language": "en",</span>
<span class="pl-s">  "debug": false</span>
<span class="pl-s">}"""</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><em>Full example: <a href="https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/python-sdk/blob/main/examples/snippets/servers/basic_resource.py">examples/snippets/servers/basic_resource.py</a></em></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tools</h3><a id="user-content-tools" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tools" href="#tools"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Tools let LLMs take actions through your server. Unlike resources, tools are expected to perform computation and have side effects:</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from mcp.server.fastmcp import FastMCP

mcp = FastMCP(name=&quot;Tool Example&quot;)


@mcp.tool()
def sum(a: int, b: int) -&gt; int:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Add two numbers together.&quot;&quot;&quot;
    return a + b


@mcp.tool()
def get_weather(city: str, unit: str = &quot;celsius&quot;) -&gt; str:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Get weather for a city.&quot;&quot;&quot;
    # This would normally call a weather API
    return f&quot;Weather in {city}: 22degrees{unit[0].upper()}&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-s1">server</span>.<span class="pl-s1">fastmcp</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">FastMCP</span>

<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">FastMCP</span>(<span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Tool Example"</span>)


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">tool</span>()</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">sum</span>(<span class="pl-s1">a</span>: <span class="pl-smi">int</span>, <span class="pl-s1">b</span>: <span class="pl-smi">int</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">int</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Add two numbers together."""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span>


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">tool</span>()</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_weather</span>(<span class="pl-s1">city</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>, <span class="pl-s1">unit</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">"celsius"</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">str</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Get weather for a city."""</span>
    <span class="pl-c"># This would normally call a weather API</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">f"Weather in <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">city</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>: 22degrees<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">unit</span>[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>].<span class="pl-c1">upper</span>()<span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><em>Full example: <a href="https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/python-sdk/blob/main/examples/snippets/servers/basic_tool.py">examples/snippets/servers/basic_tool.py</a></em></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Structured Output</h4><a id="user-content-structured-output" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Structured Output" href="#structured-output"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Tools will return structured results by default, if their return type
annotation is compatible. Otherwise, they will return unstructured results.</p>
<p dir="auto">Structured output supports these return types:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Pydantic models (BaseModel subclasses)</li>
<li>TypedDicts</li>
<li>Dataclasses and other classes with type hints</li>
<li><code>dict[str, T]</code> (where T is any JSON-serializable type)</li>
<li>Primitive types (str, int, float, bool, bytes, None) - wrapped in <code>{"result": value}</code></li>
<li>Generic types (list, tuple, Union, Optional, etc.) - wrapped in <code>{"result": value}</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Classes without type hints cannot be serialized for structured output. Only
classes with properly annotated attributes will be converted to Pydantic models
for schema generation and validation.</p>
<p dir="auto">Structured results are automatically validated against the output schema
generated from the annotation. This ensures the tool returns well-typed,
validated data that clients can easily process.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Note:</strong> For backward compatibility, unstructured results are also
returned. Unstructured results are provided for backward compatibility
with previous versions of the MCP specification, and are quirks-compatible
with previous versions of FastMCP in the current version of the SDK.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Note:</strong> In cases where a tool function's return type annotation
causes the tool to be classified as structured <em>and this is undesirable</em>,
the  classification can be suppressed by passing <code>structured_output=False</code>
to the <code>@tool</code> decorator.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from mcp.server.fastmcp import FastMCP
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
from typing import TypedDict

mcp = FastMCP(&quot;Weather Service&quot;)


# Using Pydantic models for rich structured data
class WeatherData(BaseModel):
    temperature: float = Field(description=&quot;Temperature in Celsius&quot;)
    humidity: float = Field(description=&quot;Humidity percentage&quot;)
    condition: str
    wind_speed: float


@mcp.tool()
def get_weather(city: str) -&gt; WeatherData:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Get structured weather data&quot;&quot;&quot;
    return WeatherData(
        temperature=22.5, humidity=65.0, condition=&quot;partly cloudy&quot;, wind_speed=12.3
    )


# Using TypedDict for simpler structures
class LocationInfo(TypedDict):
    latitude: float
    longitude: float
    name: str


@mcp.tool()
def get_location(address: str) -&gt; LocationInfo:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Get location coordinates&quot;&quot;&quot;
    return LocationInfo(latitude=51.5074, longitude=-0.1278, name=&quot;London, UK&quot;)


# Using dict[str, Any] for flexible schemas
@mcp.tool()
def get_statistics(data_type: str) -&gt; dict[str, float]:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Get various statistics&quot;&quot;&quot;
    return {&quot;mean&quot;: 42.5, &quot;median&quot;: 40.0, &quot;std_dev&quot;: 5.2}


# Ordinary classes with type hints work for structured output
class UserProfile:
    name: str
    age: int
    email: str | None = None

    def __init__(self, name: str, age: int, email: str | None = None):
        self.name = name
        self.age = age
        self.email = email


@mcp.tool()
def get_user(user_id: str) -&gt; UserProfile:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Get user profile - returns structured data&quot;&quot;&quot;
    return UserProfile(name=&quot;Alice&quot;, age=30, email=&quot;alice@example.com&quot;)


# Classes WITHOUT type hints cannot be used for structured output
class UntypedConfig:
    def __init__(self, setting1, setting2):
        self.setting1 = setting1
        self.setting2 = setting2


@mcp.tool()
def get_config() -&gt; UntypedConfig:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;This returns unstructured output - no schema generated&quot;&quot;&quot;
    return UntypedConfig(&quot;value1&quot;, &quot;value2&quot;)


# Lists and other types are wrapped automatically
@mcp.tool()
def list_cities() -&gt; list[str]:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Get a list of cities&quot;&quot;&quot;
    return [&quot;London&quot;, &quot;Paris&quot;, &quot;Tokyo&quot;]
    # Returns: {&quot;result&quot;: [&quot;London&quot;, &quot;Paris&quot;, &quot;Tokyo&quot;]}


@mcp.tool()
def get_temperature(city: str) -&gt; float:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Get temperature as a simple float&quot;&quot;&quot;
    return 22.5
    # Returns: {&quot;result&quot;: 22.5}"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-s1">server</span>.<span class="pl-s1">fastmcp</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">FastMCP</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">pydantic</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">BaseModel</span>, <span class="pl-v">Field</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">typing</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">TypedDict</span>

<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">FastMCP</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Weather Service"</span>)


<span class="pl-c"># Using Pydantic models for rich structured data</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">WeatherData</span>(<span class="pl-v">BaseModel</span>):
    <span class="pl-s1">temperature</span>: <span class="pl-smi">float</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">Field</span>(<span class="pl-s1">description</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Temperature in Celsius"</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">humidity</span>: <span class="pl-smi">float</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">Field</span>(<span class="pl-s1">description</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Humidity percentage"</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">condition</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">wind_speed</span>: <span class="pl-smi">float</span>


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">tool</span>()</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_weather</span>(<span class="pl-s1">city</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">WeatherData</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Get structured weather data"""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">WeatherData</span>(
        <span class="pl-s1">temperature</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">22.5</span>, <span class="pl-s1">humidity</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">65.0</span>, <span class="pl-s1">condition</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"partly cloudy"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">wind_speed</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">12.3</span>
    )


<span class="pl-c"># Using TypedDict for simpler structures</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">LocationInfo</span>(<span class="pl-v">TypedDict</span>):
    <span class="pl-s1">latitude</span>: <span class="pl-smi">float</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">longitude</span>: <span class="pl-smi">float</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">name</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">tool</span>()</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_location</span>(<span class="pl-s1">address</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">LocationInfo</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Get location coordinates"""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">LocationInfo</span>(<span class="pl-s1">latitude</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">51.5074</span>, <span class="pl-s1">longitude</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">0.1278</span>, <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"London, UK"</span>)


<span class="pl-c"># Using dict[str, Any] for flexible schemas</span>
<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">tool</span>()</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_statistics</span>(<span class="pl-s1">data_type</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">dict</span>[<span class="pl-smi">str</span>, <span class="pl-smi">float</span>]:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Get various statistics"""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> {<span class="pl-s">"mean"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">42.5</span>, <span class="pl-s">"median"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">40.0</span>, <span class="pl-s">"std_dev"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">5.2</span>}


<span class="pl-c"># Ordinary classes with type hints work for structured output</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">UserProfile</span>:
    <span class="pl-s1">name</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">age</span>: <span class="pl-smi">int</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">email</span>: <span class="pl-s1">str</span> <span class="pl-c1">|</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span>

    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">__init__</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-s1">name</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>, <span class="pl-s1">age</span>: <span class="pl-smi">int</span>, <span class="pl-s1">email</span>: <span class="pl-s1">str</span> <span class="pl-c1">|</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">age</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">age</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">email</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">email</span>


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">tool</span>()</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_user</span>(<span class="pl-s1">user_id</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">UserProfile</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Get user profile - returns structured data"""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">UserProfile</span>(<span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Alice"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">age</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">30</span>, <span class="pl-s1">email</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"alice@example.com"</span>)


<span class="pl-c"># Classes WITHOUT type hints cannot be used for structured output</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">UntypedConfig</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">__init__</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-s1">setting1</span>, <span class="pl-s1">setting2</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">setting1</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">setting1</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">setting2</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">setting2</span>


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">tool</span>()</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_config</span>() <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">UntypedConfig</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""This returns unstructured output - no schema generated"""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">UntypedConfig</span>(<span class="pl-s">"value1"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"value2"</span>)


<span class="pl-c"># Lists and other types are wrapped automatically</span>
<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">tool</span>()</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">list_cities</span>() <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">list</span>[<span class="pl-smi">str</span>]:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Get a list of cities"""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> [<span class="pl-s">"London"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"Paris"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"Tokyo"</span>]
    <span class="pl-c"># Returns: {"result": ["London", "Paris", "Tokyo"]}</span>


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">tool</span>()</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_temperature</span>(<span class="pl-s1">city</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">float</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Get temperature as a simple float"""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">22.5</span>
    <span class="pl-c"># Returns: {"result": 22.5}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Prompts</h3><a id="user-content-prompts" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Prompts" href="#prompts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Prompts are reusable templates that help LLMs interact with your server effectively:</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from mcp.server.fastmcp import FastMCP
from mcp.server.fastmcp.prompts import base

mcp = FastMCP(name=&quot;Prompt Example&quot;)


@mcp.prompt(title=&quot;Code Review&quot;)
def review_code(code: str) -&gt; str:
    return f&quot;Please review this code:\n\n{code}&quot;


@mcp.prompt(title=&quot;Debug Assistant&quot;)
def debug_error(error: str) -&gt; list[base.Message]:
    return [
        base.UserMessage(&quot;I'm seeing this error:&quot;),
        base.UserMessage(error),
        base.AssistantMessage(&quot;I'll help debug that. What have you tried so far?&quot;),
    ]"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-s1">server</span>.<span class="pl-s1">fastmcp</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">FastMCP</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-s1">server</span>.<span class="pl-s1">fastmcp</span>.<span class="pl-s1">prompts</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">base</span>

<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">FastMCP</span>(<span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Prompt Example"</span>)


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">prompt</span>(<span class="pl-s1">title</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Code Review"</span>)</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">review_code</span>(<span class="pl-s1">code</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">str</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">f"Please review this code:<span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">code</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">prompt</span>(<span class="pl-s1">title</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Debug Assistant"</span>)</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">debug_error</span>(<span class="pl-s1">error</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">list</span>[<span class="pl-s1">base</span>.<span class="pl-c1">Message</span>]:
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> [
        <span class="pl-s1">base</span>.<span class="pl-c1">UserMessage</span>(<span class="pl-s">"I'm seeing this error:"</span>),
        <span class="pl-s1">base</span>.<span class="pl-c1">UserMessage</span>(<span class="pl-s1">error</span>),
        <span class="pl-s1">base</span>.<span class="pl-c1">AssistantMessage</span>(<span class="pl-s">"I'll help debug that. What have you tried so far?"</span>),
    ]</pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Images</h3><a id="user-content-images" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Images" href="#images"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">FastMCP provides an <code>Image</code> class that automatically handles image data:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from mcp.server.fastmcp import FastMCP, Image
from PIL import Image as PILImage

mcp = FastMCP(&quot;My App&quot;)


@mcp.tool()
def create_thumbnail(image_path: str) -&gt; Image:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Create a thumbnail from an image&quot;&quot;&quot;
    img = PILImage.open(image_path)
    img.thumbnail((100, 100))
    return Image(data=img.tobytes(), format=&quot;png&quot;)"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-s1">server</span>.<span class="pl-s1">fastmcp</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">FastMCP</span>, <span class="pl-v">Image</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">create_thumbnail</span>(<span class="pl-s1">image_path</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">Image</span>:

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Context</h3><a id="user-content-context" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Context" href="#context"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Context object gives your tools and resources access to MCP capabilities:</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from mcp.server.fastmcp import Context, FastMCP

mcp = FastMCP(name=&quot;Progress Example&quot;)


@mcp.tool()
async def long_running_task(task_name: str, ctx: Context, steps: int = 5) -&gt; str:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Execute a task with progress updates.&quot;&quot;&quot;
    await ctx.info(f&quot;Starting: {task_name}&quot;)

    for i in range(steps):
        progress = (i + 1) / steps
        await ctx.report_progress(
            progress=progress,
            total=1.0,
            message=f&quot;Step {i + 1}/{steps}&quot;,
        )
        await ctx.debug(f&quot;Completed step {i + 1}&quot;)

    return f&quot;Task '{task_name}' completed&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-s1">server</span>.<span class="pl-s1">fastmcp</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">Context</span>, <span class="pl-v">FastMCP</span>

<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">FastMCP</span>(<span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Progress Example"</span>)


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">tool</span>()</span>
<span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">long_running_task</span>(<span class="pl-s1">task_name</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>, <span class="pl-s1">ctx</span>: <span class="pl-smi">Context</span>, <span class="pl-s1">steps</span>: <span class="pl-smi">int</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">str</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Execute a task with progress updates."""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">ctx</span>.<span class="pl-c1">info</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"Starting: <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">task_name</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>)

    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-s1">steps</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">progress</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">steps</span>
        <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">ctx</span>.<span class="pl-c1">report_progress</span>(
            <span class="pl-s1">progress</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">progress</span>,
            <span class="pl-s1">total</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1.0</span>,
            <span class="pl-s1">message</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">f"Step <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>/<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">steps</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>,
        )
        <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">ctx</span>.<span class="pl-c1">debug</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"Completed step <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>)

    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">f"Task '<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">task_name</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>' completed"</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><em>Full example: <a href="https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/python-sdk/blob/main/examples/snippets/servers/tool_progress.py">examples/snippets/servers/tool_progress.py</a></em></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Completions</h3><a id="user-content-completions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Completions" href="#completions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">MCP supports providing completion suggestions for prompt arguments and resource template parameters. With the context parameter, servers can provide completions based on previously resolved values:</p>
<p dir="auto">Client usage:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from mcp.client.session import ClientSession
from mcp.types import ResourceTemplateReference


async def use_completion(session: ClientSession):
    # Complete without context
    result = await session.complete(
        ref=ResourceTemplateReference(
            type=&quot;ref/resource&quot;, uri=&quot;github://repos/{owner}/{repo}&quot;
        ),
        argument={&quot;name&quot;: &quot;owner&quot;, &quot;value&quot;: &quot;model&quot;},
    )

    # Complete with context - repo suggestions based on owner
    result = await session.complete(
        ref=ResourceTemplateReference(
            type=&quot;ref/resource&quot;, uri=&quot;github://repos/{owner}/{repo}&quot;
        ),
        argument={&quot;name&quot;: &quot;repo&quot;, &quot;value&quot;: &quot;test&quot;},
        context_arguments={&quot;owner&quot;: &quot;modelcontextprotocol&quot;},
    )"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-s1">client</span>.<span class="pl-s1">session</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">ClientSession</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-s1">types</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">ResourceTemplateReference</span>


<span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">use_completion</span>(<span class="pl-s1">session</span>: <span class="pl-smi">ClientSession</span>):
    <span class="pl-c"># Complete without context</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">result</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">session</span>.<span class="pl-c1">complete</span>(
        <span class="pl-s1">ref</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">ResourceTemplateReference</span>(
            <span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"ref/resource"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">uri</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"github://repos/{owner}/{repo}"</span>
        ),
        <span class="pl-s1">argument</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>{<span class="pl-s">"name"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"owner"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"value"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"model"</span>},
    )

    <span class="pl-c"># Complete with context - repo suggestions based on owner</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">result</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">session</span>.<span class="pl-c1">complete</span>(
        <span class="pl-s1">ref</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-en">ResourceTemplateReference</span>(
            <span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"ref/resource"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">uri</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"github://repos/{owner}/{repo}"</span>
        ),
        <span class="pl-s1">argument</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>{<span class="pl-s">"name"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"repo"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"value"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"test"</span>},
        <span class="pl-s1">context_arguments</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>{<span class="pl-s">"owner"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"modelcontextprotocol"</span>},
    )</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Server implementation:</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from mcp.server.fastmcp import FastMCP
from mcp.types import (
    Completion,
    CompletionArgument,
    CompletionContext,
    PromptReference,
    ResourceTemplateReference,
)

mcp = FastMCP(name=&quot;Example&quot;)


@mcp.resource(&quot;github://repos/{owner}/{repo}&quot;)
def github_repo(owner: str, repo: str) -&gt; str:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;GitHub repository resource.&quot;&quot;&quot;
    return f&quot;Repository: {owner}/{repo}&quot;


@mcp.prompt(description=&quot;Code review prompt&quot;)
def review_code(language: str, code: str) -&gt; str:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Generate a code review.&quot;&quot;&quot;
    return f&quot;Review this {language} code:\n{code}&quot;


@mcp.completion()
async def handle_completion(
    ref: PromptReference | ResourceTemplateReference,
    argument: CompletionArgument,
    context: CompletionContext | None,
) -&gt; Completion | None:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Provide completions for prompts and resources.&quot;&quot;&quot;

    # Complete programming languages for the prompt
    if isinstance(ref, PromptReference):
        if ref.name == &quot;review_code&quot; and argument.name == &quot;language&quot;:
            languages = [&quot;python&quot;, &quot;javascript&quot;, &quot;typescript&quot;, &quot;go&quot;, &quot;rust&quot;]
            return Completion(
                values=[lang for lang in languages if lang.startswith(argument.value)],
                hasMore=False,
            )

    # Complete repository names for GitHub resources
    if isinstance(ref, ResourceTemplateReference):
        if ref.uri == &quot;github://repos/{owner}/{repo}&quot; and argument.name == &quot;repo&quot;:
            if context and context.arguments and context.arguments.get(&quot;owner&quot;) == &quot;modelcontextprotocol&quot;:
                repos = [&quot;python-sdk&quot;, &quot;typescript-sdk&quot;, &quot;specification&quot;]
                return Completion(values=repos, hasMore=False)

    return None"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-s1">server</span>.<span class="pl-s1">fastmcp</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">FastMCP</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-s1">types</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> (
    <span class="pl-v">Completion</span>,
    <span class="pl-v">CompletionArgument</span>,
    <span class="pl-v">CompletionContext</span>,
    <span class="pl-v">PromptReference</span>,
    <span class="pl-v">ResourceTemplateReference</span>,
)

<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">FastMCP</span>(<span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Example"</span>)


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">resource</span>(<span class="pl-s">"github://repos/{owner}/{repo}"</span>)</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">github_repo</span>(<span class="pl-s1">owner</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>, <span class="pl-s1">repo</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">str</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""GitHub repository resource."""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">f"Repository: <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">owner</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>/<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">repo</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">prompt</span>(<span class="pl-s1">description</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Code review prompt"</span>)</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">review_code</span>(<span class="pl-s1">language</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>, <span class="pl-s1">code</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">str</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Generate a code review."""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">f"Review this <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">language</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> code:<span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">code</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>


<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">mcp</span>.<span class="pl-c1">completion</span>()</span>
<span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">handle_completion</span>(
    <span class="pl-s1">ref</span>: <span class="pl-v">PromptReference</span> <span class="pl-c1">|</span> <span class="pl-v">ResourceTemplateReference</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">argument</span>: <span class="pl-smi">CompletionArgument</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">context</span>: <span class="pl-v">CompletionContext</span> <span class="pl-c1">|</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span>,
) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-v">Completion</span> <span class="pl-c1">|</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Provide completions for prompts and resources."""</span>

    <span class="pl-c"># Complete programming languages for the prompt</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-en">isinstance</span>(<span class="pl-s1">ref</span>, <span class="pl-v">PromptReference</span>):
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">ref</span>.<span class="pl-c1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">"review_code"</span> <span class="pl-c1">and</span> <span class="pl-s1">argument</span>.<span class="pl-c1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">"language"</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">languages</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> [<span class="pl-s">"python"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"javascript"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"typescript"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"go"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"rust"</span>]
            <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">Completion</span>(
                <span class="pl-s1">values</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[<span class="pl-s1">lang</span> <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">lang</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">languages</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">lang</span>.<span class="pl-c1">startswith</span>(<span class="pl-s1">argument</span>.<span class="pl-c1">value</span>)],
                <span class="pl-s1">hasMore</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">False</span>,
            )

    <span class="pl-c"># Complete repository names for GitHub resources</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-en">isinstance</span>(<span class="pl-s1">ref</span>, <span class="pl-v">ResourceTemplateReference</span>):
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">ref</span>.<span class="pl-c1">uri</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">"github://repos/{owner}/{repo}"</span> <span class="pl-c1">and</span> <span class="pl-s1">argument</span>.<span class="pl-c1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">"repo"</span>:
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">context</span> <span class="pl-c1">and</span> <span class="pl-s1">context</span>.<span class="pl-c1">arguments</span> <span class="pl-c1">and</span> <span class="pl-s1">context</span>.<span class="pl-c1">arguments</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"owner"</span>) <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">"modelcontextprotocol"</span>:
                <span class="pl-s1">repos</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> [<span class="pl-s">"python-sdk"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"typescript-sdk"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"specification"</span>]
                <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">Completion</span>(<span class="pl-s1">values</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">repos</span>, <span class="pl-s1">hasMore</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">False</span>)

    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><em>Full example: <a href="https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/python-sdk/blob/main/examples/snippets/servers/completion.py">examples/snippets/servers/completion.py</a></em></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Elicitation</h3><a id="user-content-elicitation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Elicitation" href="#elicitation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Request additional information from users. This example shows an Elicitation during a Tool Call:</p>
